< Text>
I was referred to Okuma through a couple of friends. This was our first time using a broker and the overall experience was excellent! The short version: the process could not be easier and I had a better feeling compared to dealing with the dealership directly after the purchase. Got a good discount and the vehicle was delivered to our home, which was very convenient! Planning on returning next time we need a vehicle!

The detailed version: Went to the company‚Äôs website and filled out an application (previous night). One of the brokers (Ken) called me back the next day asking for a few more details about what features we were looking for on the car. Also asked what dealerships we visited and if we already test drove a car (so he could make it clear to the dealer he wasn‚Äôt stealing us away from them). At the time we had a vehicle to trade in/sell. A form was e-mailed us shortly asking for some information regarding the condition of the car and a few pictures. Within a day or two, Ken called back saying there was a car available and quoted us a price that was about $3K less than sticker price. We needed some time to look into our financial details and complete the form for trading in/selling the car. After we finally analyzed our expenses, we told Ken we were willing to go through with the purchase (ended up not using Okuma to sell our car, not on them at all). Got one more call from Ken confirming details regarding delivery and telling me there was an extra option being included in on the car, no charge. < review>
I'm a big fan of getting to the airport early and not rushing thru security so I can grab a drink at the airport bar. Wasn't disappointed with my choice. I loved my breakfast sandwich for how light, yet hearty it was. Kind of hard to find that combination, in my opinion. The bread was deliciously crusty (not a soft English muffin), the egg was an egg white and there was some spinach and cheese. I ate it with a glass of champagne because I had had plenty of coffee by then. I was very full and good thing because it was around 8:30am and I was waiting on a flight from LAX to Dallas-Love. Didn't eat again until 5pm that evening. I would definitely get it again. Nice alternative to airport fast food.</review>

<gmapID>0x809442e8530737cd:0x57508c870b236bd6<//gmapID><review>First time here, I can't believe it. Beef chow fun holds a special place in my heart and I judge whether a Chinese restaurant is good or not based on how well they can cook their beef chow fun. This dish usually determines whether I'll be back or not and let me tell you, their Beef Chow Fun hit the spot. It is cooked just right where the noodles aren't mushy and stuck together in clumps. It's not overly salty. They put so many ingredients into the chow fun and with plenty of meat, whereas other places tend to be mainly noodles.

They also have Hot & Spicy sauce there too. I didn't try it but for all those Hot & Spicy lovers out there, they have it.

SAME DAY UPDATE! I was curious what else they have.

What we ordered:

Singapore Rice Noodles - this is one of my mother's favorite dish and this dish reached beyond her expectations. Again, they put a lot of different ingredient so with every bite, you always had some veggies, some pork and/or shrimp. My mom really liked that the shrimp is fried and done  so nicely.

Spicy Eggplant - Omg, it's soo good with steamed rice. It's garlicky and a little spicy, perfectly balanced. Eggplant is cooked throughly but not to the point of mush.

Garlic Green Beans - I really wanted this but they said they didn't have enough for a full order so this is a half order. If you love garlic, you should definitely try this dish (and the spicy eggplant). It's cooked perfectly where there is still that crunch when you bite into it and it's seasoned perfectly.

BBQ Pork - For the small order, it's a lot. I was afraid that it would be too fatty and sweet but it is perfect for me. It annoys me when I purchase a meat dish and for it to be mainly fat, but that is not the situation here!</review>< Time>
1607846525356< /Time>

< text>
Our usual go to Chinese spot is closed on Sunday and we were craving Chinese food and this was our first time trying Chong's.  It truly did not disappoint.  I love that they offer a variety of Asian foods.For example: You can get your Japanese/Hawaiian fix with some chicken katsu,  Thai with pad thai, or traditional chinese food where the selection is pretty extensive. I'm pretty picky with the bbq pork but they nailed it. We ordered the Chong's special friend rice and chow mein which has a little of all the protein mixed it, again, very delicious! The katsu, crispy, juicy, the way it should be. Would definitely come here again.</text>

< Text>
Not half as good since ownership change.  Very bland, won't return.

Okay, so I tried again in 2020.  Though better, the curry has a seasoning in it that does not belong, it's the same seasoning on the BBQ Pork that was way too strong as well.  Curry chicken was under cooked and pink on the outside.  I did not realize this until 3:00 in the morning when, well, let's just say trash can and toilet were both used at exact same time.  I then went straight to the fridge to check the chicken as I ate under poor lighting while watching TV and that is when I discovered the medium-rare chicken.  Special Chow Mein was not cooked long enough (though all meats were in that dish) and looked more like a Thia dish due to the amount of oil on it.  And this is coming from a dude who says "Pork Fat Rules!"  They were busy but that is no excuse to under cook food.

I was impressed with the amount of meat served in the dishes but there is still some ironing out to do.  This was my go-to Chinese food place for years until ownership changed.  I will be returning to China Restaurant which is 4 times further than Chong's.  That should speak for itself.

Just like the previous owners, this family is VERY friendly and appreciates the business.<//Text>

<review>Carl's Jr is my fav fast food burger chain. Mainly because they have different qualities of burgers from their regular to Angus. And you can get all of them without any of the multitude of toppings or a bun. The waffle fries are to die for and the real ice cream milk shakes are some of the best in the business. The chicken tenders will have you going there JUST for the chicken tenders. Every location, with the exception of the Adams Ave/Royal Palm St. one, has fast, friendly and accurate service. The Magnolia Ave/Adams Ave location has exceptional service. The Bristol St/Birch St location prompted this review where we ordered an Angus beef burger with all the veggies, no condiments, waffle fries and chicken tenders. The order was prepared quickly and perfectly. And isn't that all you really want from a fast food, burger place?< /review><Pictures>None<//Pictures><response>None</response><gmap_id>0x80dcde5474e45cab:0xe15350f3d9ba2f9c</gmap_id></record>

< review>
This place makes a really good mangonada. Very good paleteria. It was very busy when we went, but that's a really good indicator that this place is really good.

They have a really extensive range of ice cream flavors and have a good menu of snacks. I got the elote on a stick, and a large mangonada but would want to try other stuff too like tostilocos and other loaded chips.

The only downside, which isn't the store's fault, is.... the parking sucks. We had to park a couple of blocks down to get to the shop. BUT, that shouldn't stop you from getting good Mexican treats and ice cream from this place!< /review>
